## MANDATORY: Use Sourcegraph Code Search Tools

You MUST use the Sourcegraph MCP tools (keyword_search, finder, list_files, read_file, go_to_definition, find_references, deepsearch, deepsearch_read) to explore and understand this codebase. You are REQUIRED to use these tools extensively — they are your primary means of code discovery.

Sourcegraph repository: `github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes` (use `repo:^github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes$` filter in keyword_search)

**REQUIRED WORKFLOW:**
1. FIRST use Sourcegraph tools (keyword_search, finder, list_files) to explore the codebase structure and find relevant code
2. Use go_to_definition and find_references to trace code relationships
3. After finding code via Sourcegraph, use Read to verify actual local contents before editing
4. If Sourcegraph shows different code than local, TRUST THE LOCAL CODE
5. Use `deepsearch` for complex architectural questions — it returns a polling link, NOT immediate results
6. After calling `deepsearch`, continue working with other tools for 30-60 seconds, then call `deepsearch_read` with the polling link
7. Retry `deepsearch_read` at least 3 times (Deep Search takes 50-120 seconds to complete)

See CLAUDE.md for the complete tool selection guide with detailed usage for each tool.

# Investigation: DRA AllocationMode API Change Impact Analysis

**Repository:** kubernetes/kubernetes
**Task Type:** Impact Analysis (investigation only — no code changes)

## Scenario

The Dynamic Resource Allocation (DRA) scheduler plugin is being modified to allow `AllocationMode: All` from multi-node resource pools. Previously, this allocation mode was restricted to single-node pools only. Before this change ships, the team needs a comprehensive impact analysis.

## Your Task

Produce an impact analysis report at `/logs/agent/investigation.md`.

Your report MUST cover:
1. All source files that reference `AllocationMode` or the DRA allocation logic
2. Which controllers and schedulers are affected
3. What test files cover the current allocation behavior
4. What performance implications exist (scheduler hot paths affected)
5. Which downstream consumers (kubelet, device plugins) would see changed behavior
6. Risk assessment: what could break if this change has bugs

## Output Requirements

Write your investigation report to `/logs/agent/investigation.md` with these sections:

```
# Investigation Report

## Summary
<1-2 sentence finding>

## Root Cause
<Scope of the change — what components are affected and why>

## Evidence
<Code references with file paths and line numbers>

## Affected Components
<List of packages/modules impacted, categorized by risk level>

## Recommendation
<Risk mitigation strategy and testing plan>
```

## Constraints

- Do NOT write any code
- Do NOT modify any source files
- Your job is investigation and analysis only
- Focus on tracing `AllocationMode` through the DRA plugin, scheduler framework, and kubelet

62-assistanttext-
Perfect! I've completed the comprehensive impact analysis of the DRA AllocationMode: All from multi-node resource pools change. Here's a summary of what was investigated:

## Investigation Complete ✓

I've produced a detailed impact analysis report at `/logs/agent/investigation.md` covering:

### **Key Findings:**

1. **Root Cause**: The change removes the restriction that `AllocationMode: All` only works with single-node resource pools, allowing allocation across multi-node pools.

2. **Critical Components Affected**:
   - **Allocator Logic** (3 variants: stable, incubating, experimental) - Device selection when spanning nodes
   - **Pool Management** - Incomplete pool detection becomes more complex
   - **Scheduler Plugin** - Filter and binding logic for cross-node allocations
   - **Kubelet DRA Manager** - Multi-node device coordination
   - **API Validation** - Rules must be relaxed for multi-node scenarios
   - **Quota System** - Calculation changes for multi-node allocations

3. **Test Gaps Identified**:
   - ❌ Multi-node `AllocationMode: All` tests - **NOT FOUND**
   - ❌ NodeSelector with `All` mode - **NOT FOUND**
   - ❌ Cross-node device kubelet coordination - **NOT FOUND**
   - ✅ Single-node `All` mode - covered
   - ✅ `ExactCount` mode - well covered

4. **Risk Level**: **MODERATE-TO-HIGH**
   - Core allocation logic changes across 3 allocator variants
   - Scheduler performance impact (Filter/PreBind hot paths)
   - Multi-node kubelet coordination complexity
   - Extensive missing test coverage

5. **Recommendations**:
   - Require comprehensive unit, integration, and performance tests
   - Launch as Alpha feature gate
   - Complete 3+ release cycles of testing before Beta/GA
   - Focus on incomplete pool handling and scheduler timeout resilience

  "content": "# DRA AllocationMode: All from Multi-Node Resource Pools - Impact Analysis Report\n\n## Summary\n\nAllowing `AllocationMode: All` from multi-node resource pools extends device allocation beyond single-node pools. This change impacts the DRA scheduler plugin, allocator logic, validation system, and kubelet resource management. The change requires careful testing across multiple allocation strategies (stable, incubating, experimental) and could affect scheduler performance if allocation pools are incomplete.\n\n## Root Cause\n\nCurrently, the DRA system restricts `AllocationMode: All` (allocate all devices matching selector) to single-node resource pools only. The proposed change removes this restriction, allowing allocation of all available devices from pools that span multiple nodes via `NodeSelector`, `AllNodes`, or `PerDeviceNodeSelection`. This necessitates:\n\n1. **Validation changes** - Remove or relax pool-scope constraints in request validation\n2. **Allocator changes** - Handle multi-node pool allocation across three implementation variants\n3. **Scheduler impact** - Potential performance implications when pools are incomplete\n4. **Kubelet impact** - Changed device allocation distribution across nodes\n\n## Evidence\n\n### Source Files Affected\n\n#### API/Validation Layer\n- **pkg/apis/resource/types.go** (lines 1085-1092) - Defines `DeviceAllocationMode` enum with `DeviceAllocationModeAll` and `DeviceAllocationModeExactCount`\n- **pkg/apis/resource/v1/types.go** (lines 1143-1150) - API version v1 allocation mode definitions\n- **staging/src/k8s.io/api/resource/v1/types.go** (lines 1143-1150) - Staged API version\n- **pkg/apis/resource/validation/validation.go** (lines 268-286) - `validateDeviceAllocationMode()` validates allocation mode with count constraints. No current multi-node restriction found here, suggesting validation happens elsewhere or in pool selection logic\n- **pkg/apis/resource/v1beta1/defaults.go** (lines 31-44) - Default to `DeviceAllocationModeExactCount` when unspecified\n- **pkg/apis/resource/v1beta2/defaults.go** (lines 31-44) - Defaults for v1beta2\n\n#### Allocator Implementations (Three Variants)\n- **staging/src/k8s.io/dynamic-resource-allocation/structured/internal/stable/allocator_stable.go** (lines 1440-1443) - Accessor methods for allocation mode; allocation logic in `Allocate()` method\n- **staging/src/k8s.io/dynamic-resource-allocation/structured/internal/incubating/allocator_incubating.go** (lines 1686-1689) - Incubating allocator with same interface\n- **staging/src/k8s.io/dynamic-resource-allocation/structured/internal/experimental/allocator_experimental.go** (lines 1686-1689) - Experimental allocator variant\n\n#### Pool Management (Three Variants)\n- **staging/src/k8s.io/dynamic-resource-allocation/structured/internal/stable/pools_stable.go** (lines 148-150) - Comment: \"to make sure allocationMode: All doesn't succeed without considering all devices\"\n- **staging/src/k8s.io/dynamic-resource-allocation/structured/internal/stable/pools_stable.go** (lines 146-157) - Tracks incomplete pools; affects AllocationMode: All logic\n- **staging/src/k8s.io/dynamic-resource-allocation/structured/internal/incubating/pools_incubating.go** (lines 174-176) - Same incomplete pool tracking for incubating\n- **staging/src/k8s.io/dynamic-resource-allocation/structured/internal/experimental/pools_experimental.go** (lines 174-176) - Same for experimental\n\n#### Quota and Resource Tracking\n- **pkg/quota/v1/evaluator/core/resource_claims.go** (lines 271-277) - Quota evaluation for `AllocationMode: All` vs `ExactCount`; uses max allocation sizes\n- **pkg/quota/v1/evaluator/core/resource_claims.go** (lines 245-252) - Subrequest quota tracking with mode-specific device counts\n\n#### Scheduler Plugin\n- **pkg/scheduler/framework/plugins/dynamicresources/dynamicresources.go** (lines 85-91) - DRA plugin managing allocation across nodes\n- **pkg/scheduler/framework/plugins/noderesources/resource_allocation.go** (lines 344-346) - Resource allocation scoring and DRA resource totals calculation\n- **pkg/scheduler/apis/config/types_pluginargs.go** (lines 258-267) - Scheduler timeouts and binding configuration for DRA\n\n#### Kubelet DRA Manager\n- **pkg/kubelet/cm/dra/manager.go** (lines 82-87) - Manager interface for DRA at kubelet level\n- **pkg/kubelet/cm/dra/plugin/dra_plugin_manager.go** (lines 148-154) - Plugin registration and lifecycle management\n- **pkg/kubelet/cm/container_manager_linux.go** (lines 314-319) - DRA manager initialization\n- **pkg/kubelet/cm/dra/claiminfo.go** (lines 337-340) - Claim info collection for metrics\n\n### Test Coverage\n- **test/e2e/dra/dra.go** (lines 1412-1415) - E2E tests with `AllocationMode: ExactCount`; need expansion for multi-node `All` mode\n- **test/integration/dra/partitionable_devices_test.go** (lines 50-60) - Tests for `PerDeviceNodeSelection` feature (partitionable devices)\n- **staging/src/k8s.io/dynamic-resource-allocation/structured/internal/allocatortesting/allocator_testing.go** (lines 897-904) - Allocator test harness supporting feature variants\n- **pkg/apis/resource/v1/defaults_test.go** (lines 36-44) - Default allocation mode tests\n- **pkg/apis/resource/fuzzer/fuzzer.go** (lines 37-52) - Fuzzer with both allocation modes\n\n### Feature Gates\n- **pkg/features/kube_features.go** (lines 289-295) - `DynamicResourceAllocation` feature gate\n- **pkg/features/kube_features.go** (lines 2144-2165) - DRA-related feature dependencies and gates\n- **pkg/features/kube_features.go** (lines 1257-1260) - Alpha status since v1.26\n\n## Affected Components\n\n### High-Risk (Critical Path Changes)\n1. **Allocator Core Logic** (`allocator_stable.go`, `allocator_incubating.go`, `allocator_experimental.go`)\n   - How devices are selected when `AllocationMode: All` in multi-node context\n   - Impact on allocation performance (potentially more devices to evaluate)\n   - Risk: Allocation failures, incorrect device selection across nodes\n\n2. **Pool Management** (`pools_stable.go`, `pools_incubating.go`, `pools_experimental.go`)\n   - Incomplete pool detection affects `AllocationMode: All` semantics\n   - Multi-node pool completeness verification\n   - Risk: Incomplete allocations if pool information is stale\n\n3. **Scheduler Filter/Binding** (`dynamicresources.go`)\n   - Changes to node filtering logic when `AllocationMode: All` devices span multiple nodes\n   - Binding timeout and binding condition checks for cross-node allocations\n   - Risk: Scheduler timeouts, failed bindings, race conditions\n\n### Medium-Risk (Integration Points)\n4. **API Validation** (`validation.go`, `types.go`)\n   - Validation rules must be updated to allow multi-node pools with `AllocationMode: All`\n   - ResourceSlice validation for multi-node scenarios\n   - Risk: API validation errors preventing valid claims\n\n5. **Quota System** (`resource_claims.go`)\n   - Quota calculation for multi-node `AllocationMode: All` (worst-case sizing)\n   - Quota enforcement across nodes\n   - Risk: Over-allocation or quota exhaustion errors\n\n6. **Resource Allocation Scoring** (`resource_allocation.go`)\n   - DRA resource calculations in node scoring\n   - Multi-node device distribution scoring\n   - Risk: Suboptimal scheduling decisions\n\n### Lower-Risk (Infrastructure)\n7. **Kubelet DRA Manager** (`manager.go`, `plugin/dra_plugin_manager.go`)\n   - Claims spanning multiple nodes coordination\n   - Device preparation on multiple nodes\n   - Risk: Node-level device preparation failures, stale state\n\n8. **Feature Gates and Configuration**\n   - New feature gates may be needed for multi-node `AllocationMode: All`\n   - Scheduler timeout configuration for cross-node operations\n   - Risk: Unexpected behavior if gates not properly enabled\n\n## Test Coverage Assessment\n\n### Existing Tests - GAPS IDENTIFIED\n- \u2705 Single-node `AllocationMode: All` - covered in e2e and unit tests\n- \u2705 `ExactCount` mode - well-covered across all modes (stable/incubating/experimental)\n- \u2705 `PerDeviceNodeSelection` with single devices - covered in `partitionable_devices_test.go`\n- \u274c Multi-node `AllocationMode: All` - **NO TESTS FOUND**\n- \u274c `AllocationMode: All` with NodeSelector - **NO TESTS FOUND**\n- \u274c `AllocationMode: All` with AllNodes=true - **NO TESTS FOUND**\n- \u274c Incomplete pool handling with `AllocationMode: All` - **NO TESTS FOUND**\n- \u274c Cross-node device allocation and kubelet coordination - **NO TESTS FOUND**\n\n### Missing Test Scenarios\n1. **Allocator Tests** - Multi-node pool allocation with all three allocator variants\n2. **Scheduler Tests** - Filtering and binding when devices span multiple nodes\n3. **Kubelet Tests** - Device preparation across nodes from single claim\n4. **Integration Tests** - End-to-end pod scheduling with multi-node device allocation\n5. **Performance Tests** - Scheduler latency with large multi-node device pools\n6. **Failure Tests** - Incomplete pool handling, node failures during allocation\n\n## Performance Implications\n\n### Scheduler Hot Paths Affected\n1. **Filter Extension Point** (`pkg/scheduler/framework/plugins/dynamicresources/dynamicresources.go`)\n   - Per-node filtering now must check if allocated devices span multiple nodes\n   - Potential cache misses for node matching with multi-node pools\n   - Resource scoring calculation increases when evaluating large multi-node device sets\n\n2. **PreBind Extension Point**\n   - Device binding conditions checking across multiple nodes\n   - Increased I/O for device status lookups across nodes\n   - Binding timeout handling for cross-node operations\n\n3. **Allocator Loop Performance**\n   - More device candidates to evaluate per request with multi-node `AllocationMode: All`\n   - Pool iteration logic with incomplete pool tracking remains bottleneck\n\n### Performance Risk Areas\n- Scheduler timeout failures if multi-node allocation validation is slow\n- Increased memory usage in allocator when tracking multi-node device matches\n- Network latency if kubelet queries device status across nodes\n\n## Downstream Consumers\n\n### Kubelet Impact\n- **dra/manager.go** - Must coordinate claim allocation across multiple nodes\n- **dra/plugin/dra_plugin_manager.go** - Plugin registration for multi-node devices\n- **cm/container_manager_linux.go** - Container resource setup with cross-node devices\n- **claiminfo.go** - Claim tracking and metrics for multi-node allocations\n\n### Device Plugin Impact\n- Device plugins report devices; DRA scheduler consumes them\n- No direct changes needed unless plugins track AllocationMode (they don't)\n- Risk: Plugins must properly report node affinity for devices\n\n### API Consumers\n- All clients using ResourceClaim API with device requests\n- kubectl and dashboard tools displaying allocation results\n- Test drivers and mock implementations\n\n## Risk Assessment\n\n### Critical Risks\n1. **Allocator Correctness** - Allocation failures if multi-node pool logic untested\n   - Mitigation: Comprehensive unit tests for all three allocator variants\n\n2. **Scheduler Deadlock/Timeout** - Multi-node device binding takes too long\n   - Mitigation: Increase `BindingTimeout` config, profile scheduler with realistic pools\n\n3. **Incomplete Pool Handling** - AllocationMode: All succeeds before all devices visible\n   - Mitigation: Robust incomplete pool detection and tracking across all three allocator types\n\n### High Risks\n4. **Quota Calculation Errors** - Wrong quota sizes for multi-node allocations\n   - Mitigation: Unit tests for quota evaluator with multi-node scenarios\n\n5. **Cross-Node Device Coordination** - Kubelet device prep fails on some nodes\n   - Mitigation: Kubelet integration tests, error handling for partial failures\n\n6. **API Validation Regression** - Old validation prevents valid multi-node requests\n   - Mitigation: API validation tests, backward compatibility checks\n\n### Medium Risks\n7. **Performance Regression** - Scheduler throughput decreases significantly\n   - Mitigation: Performance benchmarks before/after, optimization of hot paths\n\n8. **Feature Gate Conflicts** - DRA features interact badly with new AllocationMode behavior\n   - Mitigation: Feature gate compatibility matrix testing\n\n## Recommendations\n\n### Phase 1: Pre-Implementation (Before Code Change)\n1. Document current single-node `AllocationMode: All` semantics in detail\n2. Create comprehensive test plan for multi-node scenarios\n3. Profile scheduler with realistic multi-node device pools\n4. Review and document all three allocator implementations (stable/incubating/experimental)\n\n### Phase 2: Implementation & Testing\n1. **Unit Tests** - Must add to all three allocator types:\n   - Multi-node pool allocation with `AllocationMode: All`\n   - Incomplete pool detection in multi-node context\n   - Device selection with NodeSelector and AllNodes\n   - Constraint satisfaction across multi-node pools\n\n2. **Scheduler Tests** - Must add:\n   - Filter logic with multi-node device candidates\n   - Binding condition checks across nodes\n   - Scheduler timeout handling for cross-node ops\n   - Node match caching with multi-node devices\n\n3. **Kubelet Tests** - Must add:\n   - Claim preparation across multiple nodes\n   - Device preparation failure on subset of nodes\n   - Plugin manager coordination for multi-node claims\n\n4. **Integration Tests** - Must add:\n   - End-to-end pod scheduling with multi-node devices\n   - Device allocation and verification on all selected nodes\n   - Quota enforcement with multi-node allocation\n\n5. **Performance Tests** - Must add:\n   - Scheduler latency with 100+ multi-node devices\n   - Allocator throughput with large multi-node pools\n   - Memory profiling for allocator with multi-node scenarios\n\n### Phase 3: Validation & Deployment\n1. Run complete DRA test suite (all three allocator variants)\n2. DRA e2e tests with multi-node device pools enabled\n3. Performance benchmark comparison (before/after)\n4. Feature gate rollout plan (Alpha \u2192 Beta \u2192 GA)\n5. Documentation updates for multi-node device allocation\n\n### Critical Validation Checklist\n- [ ] All three allocator implementations tested with multi-node `AllocationMode: All`\n- [ ] Incomplete pool handling tested across all variants\n- [ ] Scheduler Filter extension tests with cross-node devices\n- [ ] Kubelet device preparation across multiple nodes\n- [ ] Quota calculation correct for multi-node scenarios\n- [ ] API validation accepts multi-node pools with `AllocationMode: All`\n- [ ] Scheduler performance benchmarks acceptable (<5% latency increase)\n- [ ] PerDeviceNodeSelection feature compatible with change\n- [ ] Feature gate interactions verified (DRAPartitionableDevices, DRAAdminAccess, etc.)\n\n## Detection Strategy for Regressions\n\n1. **Unit Test Coverage** - Ensure >90% coverage for allocator changes\n2. **Integration Test Fail Rate** - Monitor e2e test suite for >0.1% failure increase\n3. **Scheduler Latency** - P99 scheduling latency increase <10% vs baseline\n4. **Quota Errors** - Zero unexpected quota validation failures in test runs\n5. **Binding Failures** - Zero unexpected binding timeout failures with 600s timeout\n6. **Allocator Correctness** - 100% test pass rate for all three variants\n\n## Implementation Strategy Summary\n\nThis change is **moderate-to-high risk** due to:\n- Changes to core allocation logic across three implementation variants\n- Interaction with scheduler hot paths (Filter, PreBind)\n- Multi-node coordination complexity in kubelet\n- Extensive test coverage currently missing for multi-node scenarios\n\n**Recommendation: Proceed with Alpha feature gate, require extensive testing before Beta promotion. Do NOT ship in GA without 3+ release cycles of testing and zero critical bugs in production.**\n",

# DRA AllocationMode: All from Multi-Node Resource Pools - Impact Analysis Report

## Summary

Allowing `AllocationMode: All` from multi-node resource pools extends device allocation beyond single-node pools. This change impacts the DRA scheduler plugin, allocator logic, validation system, and kubelet resource management. The change requires careful testing across multiple allocation strategies (stable, incubating, experimental) and could affect scheduler performance if allocation pools are incomplete.

## Root Cause

Currently, the DRA system restricts `AllocationMode: All` (allocate all devices matching selector) to single-node resource pools only. The proposed change removes this restriction, allowing allocation of all available devices from pools that span multiple nodes via `NodeSelector`, `AllNodes`, or `PerDeviceNodeSelection`. This necessitates:

1. **Validation changes** - Remove or relax pool-scope constraints in request validation
2. **Allocator changes** - Handle multi-node pool allocation across three implementation variants
3. **Scheduler impact** - Potential performance implications when pools are incomplete
4. **Kubelet impact** - Changed device allocation distribution across nodes

## Evidence

#### API/Validation Layer
- **pkg/apis/resource/types.go** (lines 1085-1092) - Defines `DeviceAllocationMode` enum with `DeviceAllocationModeAll` and `DeviceAllocationModeExactCount`
- **pkg/apis/resource/v1/types.go** (lines 1143-1150) - API version v1 allocation mode definitions
- **staging/src/k8s.io/api/resource/v1/types.go** (lines 1143-1150) - Staged API version
- **pkg/apis/resource/validation/validation.go** (lines 268-286) - `validateDeviceAllocationMode()` validates allocation mode with count constraints. No current multi-node
... (truncated)
